Comparison of $mol with other frameworks in the js-framework-benchmark.

$mol implementation: sources, online.

Results

- $mol guarantees instant operation regardless of the amount of data.

- Memory consumption on $mol at the level of the most compact low-level solutions.

Notice

- $mol is high level application framework. Most others - low level UI frameworks.

- $mol uses automatic rendering virtualization. Others don't support that.
